摘要翻译

量子相干性及其他非经典特征在化学动力学中被广泛讨论，但如何量化这些资源在特定过程和观测量中的操作相关性仍存在困难。尽管量子资源理论为比较自由场景与资源场景提供了完备框架，现有方法通常依赖于资源单调量或自由操作下的性能界限，并未直接量化选定资源对固定化学动力学过程所能产生的最大影响。本文引入任务特定、过程层面的量化指标，用以界定量子资源对目标品质因数可能引发的最大变化上限。其核心是资源影响泛函 $\mathcal{C}_M(Λ)$，该泛函通过比较同一量子通道 $Λ$ 作用下量子态与其配对的资源无关对应态来定义，并可在二元假设检验中获得操作化诠释。我们推导了约束资源改变目标信号速率的变分界限与时间界限，提供了量子速度极限的资源感知类比。此外，我们证明开放系统动力学可分解为自由分量与资源分量，使得仅有资源分量对 $\mathcal{C}_M(Λ)$ 产生贡献，从而分离出生成元中导致可观测量发生资源诱导变化的部分。我们通过供体-受体二聚体在两种可解析求解体系中的能量转移过程，示例性阐释了该框架的应用。本研究为诊断和标定分子过程中的量子资源效应提供了一套通用工具箱。

Abstract

Quantum coherence and other non-classical features are widely discussed in chemical dynamics, yet it remains difficult to quantify when such resources are operationally relevant for a given process and observable. While quantum resource theories provide a comprehensive framework for comparing free and resourceful settings, existing approaches typically rely on resource monotones or on performance bounds under free operations, and do not directly quantify the maximal influence a chosen resource can exert on a fixed chemical dynamics. Here, we introduce task specific, process level quantifiers that upper bound the largest change a quantum resource can induce in a target figure of merit. Central is a resource impact functional $\mathcal{C}_M(Λ)$, defined by comparing a state with its paired resource-free counterpart under the same quantum channel $Λ$, which admits an operational interpretation in binary hypothesis testing. We derive variation and time bounds that constrain how rapidly a resource can modify a target signal, providing resource-aware analogues of quantum speed limits. Moreover, we show that open system dynamics can be decomposed into free and resourceful components such that only the resourceful component contributes to $\mathcal{C}_M(Λ)$, thereby isolating the parts of a generator responsible for resource-induced changes in the observable. We illustrate the framework exemplary for energy transfer in a donor-acceptor dimer in two analytically solvable regimes. Our results provide a general toolbox for diagnosing and benchmarking quantum resource effects in molecular processes.

Authors: Ramesh Radhakrishnan, Gerald Cleaver, William Julius
Published: 2026-03-06
TL;DR: 该论文研究了旋转Teo虫洞中质量less标量扰动的量子场论处理，通过Bogoliubov变换计算了粒子产生和纠缠熵，发现旋转和框架拖拽导致几何不对称性，产生类似于非对称动态卡西米尔效应的静止粒子创造机制。
摘要翻译

旋转可穿越虫洞使得我们能够在没有事件视界的情况下研究参考系拖曳与旋转效应。本文发展了旋转Teo时空背景下无质量标量扰动的量子场论处理方法。该时空是一个精确、稳态、无视界的虫洞解，连接两个渐进平直区域。利用Bogoliubov变换形式体系，我们在两个渐进区域上构建了“入”态和“出”态模解，并计算了用于量化真空模混合的Bogoliubov系数。 由旋转和参考系拖曳诱导的有效径向势垒形成了一个非对称散射势垒。这种几何非对称性使得我们可以通过势垒穿透指数精确解析地计算反射和透射振幅，从而得到了Bogoliubov系数、平均粒子数以及双模纠缠熵关于旋转参数的闭合表达式。由此产生的放大效应源于量子Bogoliubov模混合与真空压缩，而非经典意义上的超辐射通量增强。 由于该时空是稳态的，粒子产生源自几何非对称性与边界条件，而非显式的时间依赖性。共转模与反共转模经历不等价的散射过程，这导致该过程本质上是非互易的。我们将此机制识别为一种稳态的、几何意义上的非对称动力学卡西米尔效应（Asymmetric Dynamical Casimir Effect, ADCE）类比。在旋转Teo几何中，旋转与参考系拖曳扮演了动力学卡西米尔效应中运动边界所扮演的角色，成为非对称真空模混合的根源。

Abstract

Rotating traversable wormholes allow the effects of frame dragging and rotation to be studied in the absence of event horizons. We develop a quantum field theoretic treatment of massless scalar perturbations in the rotating Teo spacetime. This spacetime is an exact, stationary, horizonless wormhole connecting two asymptotically flat regions. Using the Bogoliubov transformation formalism, we construct ``in'' and ``out'' mode solutions defined on the two asymptotic regions and compute the Bogoliubov coefficients that quantify vacuum mode mixing. The effective radial potential induced by rotation and frame dragging forms an asymmetric scattering barrier. This geometric asymmetry allows an exact analytic evaluation of reflection and transmission amplitudes via the barrier-penetration exponent. This results in closed-form expressions for the Bogoliubov coefficients, the mean particle number, and the two-mode entanglement entropy as functions of the rotation parameter. The resulting amplification arises at the level of quantum Bogoliubov mode mixing and vacuum squeezing, rather than classical superradiant flux enhancement. Since this spacetime is stationary, particle creation originates from geometric asymmetry and boundary conditions, and not from explicit time dependence. Co-rotating and counter-rotating modes experience inequivalent scattering. This renders the process intrinsically non-reciprocal. We identify this mechanism as a stationary, geometric analogue of the Asymmetric Dynamical Casimir Effect (ADCE). In the rotating Teo geometry, rotation and frame dragging play the role that moving boundaries play in the dynamical Casimir effect, acting as the source of asymmetric vacuum mode mixing.

59. Heterogeneous quantum error-correcting codes FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 14.0
Authors: Omid Khosravani, Guillermo Escobar-Arrieta, Kenneth R. Brown, Mauricio Gutierrez
Published: 2026-03-06
TL;DR: 该研究提出了由不同噪声特性的量子比特组成的异质量子纠错码，通过优化量子比特布局策略，显著提高了纠错阈值并降低了逻辑错误率。
摘要翻译

我们提出了一种由具有不同错误通道的量子比特类型构成的异质量子纠错码，并采用最大似然张量网络解码方法研究了其在码容量机制下的性能。在两种量子比特类型共享相同噪声偏置但物理错误率不同的情况下，将噪声较高的量子比特置于体区（其中每个错误会触发更多校验位），而将较清洁的量子比特置于边界，可使阈值超过0.4（相比之下，反向布局的阈值约为0.2），并在高偏置条件下将逻辑错误率降低超过三个数量级，且该优势随码距呈指数增长。在两种类型共享相同错误率但偏置不同的情况下，最优策略发生逆转：将高偏置（更可预测）量子比特置于边界，可将阈值在偏置比为100时从0.292(5)提升至0.360(9)，在偏置比为1000时从0.29(1)提升至0.398(4)。我们还观察到一个显著的偏置反转特性：尽管物理噪声是ZZ（Z方向）偏置的，逻辑错误通道却呈现出强烈的XX（X方向）和YY（Y方向）偏置。我们提出了一个稳定子比率假说，为两种布局规则提供了统一的信息论解释，并预测在颜色码等码族中该优势将进一步扩大。

Abstract

We introduce heterogeneous quantum error-correcting codes composed of qubit types with distinct error channels and study their performance in the code-capacity regime using maximum-likelihood tensor network decoding. In the regime where both qubit types share the same noise bias but differ in physical error rate, placing noisier qubits in the bulk -- where each error triggers more syndrome bits -- and cleaner qubits on the boundary yields thresholds exceeding 0.4 (compared to ~0.2 for the reverse placement) and improvements exceeding three orders of magnitude in logical error rate at high bias, with the advantage growing exponentially with code distance. In the regime where both types share the same error rate but differ in bias, the optimal strategy reverses: placing high-bias (more predictable) qubits on the boundary increases the threshold from 0.292(5) to 0.360(9) at a bias ratio of 100, and from 0.29(1) to 0.398(4) at a bias ratio of 1000. We also observe a striking bias-inversion property: the logical error channel becomes strongly XX X- and YY Y-biased despite the physical noise being ZZ Z-biased. We propose a stabilizer-ratio hypothesis that provides a unified information-theoretic explanation for both placement rules and predicts even larger advantages for code families such as color codes.

60. Enhancing superconductivity using thermal bosons FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 14.0
Authors: Ekaterina Vlasiuk, Manfred Salmhofer, Eugene Demler, Richard Schmidt
Published: 2026-03-06
TL;DR: 该研究探讨了超导体与热玻色子的强耦合如何提高其超导临界温度，并建立了由玻色子驱动的增强超导相图。
摘要翻译

本研究探讨了超导体与热玻色子的强耦合如何提升其超导临界温度。为解决该问题，我们采用重正化群方法，该方法能够描述密度涨落与玻色子诱导的费米子间吸引力建立之间的竞争关系。通过捕捉玻色子与费米子领域的相互影响，自洽重正化群框架预测了在广泛相互作用范围内临界温度的显著提升。我们发现临界温度对玻色子质量存在非平庸的依赖关系，并建立了由凝聚态或热态玻色子驱动的增强超导性的相图。我们概述了在冷原子系统中可能的实验实现方案，并讨论了利用范德瓦尔斯材料异质结构中的电子-激子混合体系的具体实施方案。

Abstract

We investigate how the strong coupling of a superconductor to thermal bosons can enhance its superconducting critical temperature. To tackle this problem, we use a renormalization group approach that allows us to describe the competition between density fluctuations and the build-up of boson-induced attraction between fermions. Capturing the mutual influence of bosonic and fermionic sectors, the self-consistent renormalization group framework predicts a robust increase of the critical temperature across a wide range of interactions. We find a nontrivial dependence of the critical temperature on the boson mass and we establish a phase diagram for enhanced superconductivity driven by bosons being either in the condensed or thermal state. We outline possible experimental realizations in cold atomic systems and discuss implementations using electron-exciton mixtures in van der Waals material heterostructures.

61. An ode to instantons FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 14.0
Authors: Oliver Janssen, Joel Karlsson, Flavio Riccardi, Mattia Varrone
Published: 2026-03-06
TL;DR: 该论文研究了量子力学中半经典时间演化的形式化方法，通过识别不同时间域中的鞍点来解决亚稳态衰变问题，旨在为量子场论中具有非平凡时间依赖性的衰变率计算提供理论基础。
摘要翻译

我们提出了一种基于百年研究积累的量子力学半经典时间演化形式体系。该体系识别了实时间中的复鞍点、复时间中的实鞍点以及复时间中的复鞍点，这些鞍点在经典问题中重现了已知结果。针对亚稳态的衰变过程，我们发现了有限时间和有限能量下与“反弹解”类似的对应结构，这些结构并不具有严格的零模或负模。文中讨论了波函数的一圈相位以及晚期反弹解的多重性问题。本研究的动机在于，通过首先回归至引人入胜的量子力学领域进行基础探索，以掌握如何在具有非平庸时间依赖性的量子场论情景中计算衰变速率。

Abstract

We present a formalism for semiclassical time evolution in quantum mechanics, building on a century of work. We identify complex saddle points in real time, real saddle points in complex time, and complex saddle points in complex time that reproduce the known answers in classic problems. For the decay of a metastable state, we find finite time and finite energy analogs of the "bounce" which do not have strict zero or negative modes. The one-loop phase of the wave function and the multiplicity of bounce solutions at late times are discussed. The motivation of this work is to learn how to compute decay rates in quantum field theory in situations with non-trivial time dependence, by first taking a humble step backwards to the fascinating world of quantum mechanics.

62. Quantum Technologies and Edge Devices in Electrical Grids: Opportunities, Challenges, and Future Directions FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 14.0
Authors: Marjorie Hoegen, René Glebke, M. Sahnawaz Alam, Alessandro David, Juan Navarro Arenas, Nikolaus Wirtz, Mario Albanese, Daniele Carta, Felix Motzoi, Antonello Monti, Carsten Schuck, Andrea Benigni, Klaus Wehrle, Ferdinanda Ponci
Published: 2026-03-06
TL;DR: 该论文探讨了量子技术如何解决电力系统边缘设备在计算能力、传感精度和通信安全方面的局限性，并分析了量子计算、量子传感器和量子通信在电网中的集成机会与挑战。
摘要翻译

在现代电力系统中，边缘设备作为本地枢纽，负责数据采集、现场计算、电气参数感知、控制指令执行以及与相邻边缘设备的通信，共同构成大规模电网的组成部分。然而，随着监测节点和控制回路数量的增长，传统边缘设备面临严峻限制。复杂的信号处理与决策任务可能导致设备过载，引发延迟和能耗上升。标准传感器受限于噪声基底，难以检测微小变化，使得故障或不稳定早期征兆的识别更为困难。同时，传统通信链路受带宽限制、安全风险和日益增长的加密需求制约，这些因素共同减缓并削弱了关键电网信息的传输。量子技术有望突破这些瓶颈。量子计算机能够为传统处理器无法处理的优化和机器学习任务提供指数级加速；量子传感器可实现原子级精度的信号感知，赋予边缘设备更精确的电网动态观测能力；包括量子密钥分发在内的量子通信技术，为实现信息论安全提供了途径，确保信息快速且无篡改地传输。本文探讨了量子技术融入边缘设备的可行路径，并着重分析了其机遇与挑战。

Abstract

In modern power systems, edge devices serve as local hubs that collect data, perform on-site computing, sense electrical parameters, execute control actions, and communicate with neighboring edge devices as part of the larger grid. However, as the number of monitored nodes and control loops grows, traditional edge devices face serious limits. They can become overloaded by complex signal processing and decision tasks, causing delays and higher energy use. Standard sensors hit a noise floor that prevents them from detecting miniature changes, making it harder to spot early signs of faults or instability. Meanwhile, conventional communication links struggle with bandwidth limits, security risks, and rising encryption demands, which together slow down and weaken the transfer of critical grid information. Quantum technologies have the potential to overcome these challenges. Quantum computers can deliver exponential speed-ups for optimization and machine-learning tasks that ordinary processors cannot handle. Quantum sensors can sense signals with atomic precision, giving edge devices a more precise view of grid dynamics. Quantum communication techniques, including quantum key distribution, offer methods to achieve information-theoretic security and ensure that information arrives quickly and without tampering. We explore how quantum technologies can be integrated into edge devices, highlighting both opportunities and challenges.

63. Radio-Frequency Side-Channel Analysis of a Trapped-Ion Quantum Computer FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 14.0
Authors: Giorgio Grigolo, Dorian Schiffer, Lukas Gerster, Martin Ringbauer, Paul Erker
Published: 2026-03-06
TL;DR: 该论文研究囚禁离子量子计算机中射频信号泄漏导致的侧信道攻击，通过现成组件检测并提取了量子门脉冲特征，证明了这一新型攻击向量的可行性，并提出了缓解信息泄漏的方法。
摘要翻译

与经典计算机类似，量子处理器也存在侧信道，可能使攻击者获取潜在的专有算法。我们识别并利用了一种在囚禁离子量子处理器中先前未被探索的侧信道，该信道源于用于调制离子冷却、门操作和读取的激光的射频（RF）信号。在这些量子处理器中，声光调制器（AOMs）将相位和频率调制施加到与离子相互作用的激光场上，以实现个体和集体幺正操作。AOMs由强射频信号驱动，其中一部分信号会从设备中泄漏。我们讨论了利用此侧信道的一般策略，并演示了如何使用现成组件检测基于最先进qudit量子处理器的射频泄漏。从这些数据中，我们提取了单离子门和纠缠门的脉冲特征，从而实现了对这一新型攻击载体的原理性利用验证。最后，我们概述了通过该侧信道缓解信息泄漏的方法。

Abstract

Analogously to classical computers, quantum processors exhibit side channels that may give attackers access to potentially proprietary algorithms. We identify and exploit a previously unexplored side channel in trapped-ion quantum processors that arises from the radio-frequency (RF) signals used to modulate lasers for ion cooling, gate execution, and readout. In these quantum processors, acousto-optical modulators (AOMs) imprint phase and frequency modulations onto laser fields interacting with the ions to implement individual and collective unitaries. The AOMs are driven by strong RF signals, a fraction of which leaks out of the device. We discuss general strategies to exploit this side channel and demonstrate how to detect RF leakage from a state-of-the-art qudit-based quantum processor using off-the-shelf components. From this data, we extract pulse characteristics of single-ion and entangling gates, thereby implementing a proof-of-principle exploitation of the novel attack vector. Finally, we outline ways to mitigate the information leakage through the presented side channel.

64. An Atomic Interface for High-Dimensional Temporal Mode Quantum Networks FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 14.0
Authors: Shicheng Zhang, Aonan Zhang, Ilse Maillette de Buy Wenniger, Paul M. Burdekin, Jerzy Szuniewicz, Steven Sagona-Stophel, Sarah E. Thomas, Ian A. Walmsley
Published: 2026-03-06
TL;DR: 该论文解决了高维量子网络中光子时间模式的同步、处理和接口问题，通过使用热铯蒸气中的拉曼量子存储器，实现了可编程的高维时间模式处理器，能够选择性地存储、过滤和转换MHz与GHz带宽模式之间的相干接口。
摘要翻译

光子的时间模式因其高信道容量和光纤兼容性，成为高维量子网络中极具前景的编码方案。然而，要充分发挥其潜力，需要能够在光子与原子带宽之间对这些模式进行同步、处理和接口连接的设备。本工作中，我们利用温铯蒸气中的拉曼量子存储器，展示了一种可编程的高维时间模式处理器。我们利用拉曼相互作用核的单模特性，通过动态整形控制场，合成了一种可调谐的相干滤波器，能够选择性地寻址特定的时间波形。这一机制实现了按需的存储、滤波和转换，为MHz与GHz带宽模式之间提供了相干接口。我们在30个正交厄米-高斯模式构成的基上验证了该平台的模式选择性，并通过5维量子过程层析技术认证了其高保真度的量子操作。通过将确定性模式转换与双向带宽接口相结合，我们确立了拉曼存储器作为可扩展量子信息处理的关键主动节点。

Abstract

Temporal modes of photons are a promising encoding scheme for high-dimensional quantum networks due to their high channel capacity and fiber compatibility. However, realizing their full potential requires devices capable of synchronizing, processing and interfacing these modes across photonic and atomic bandwidths. In this work, we demonstrate a programmable high-dimensional temporal mode processor using a Raman quantum memory in warm cesium vapor. We exploit the single-mode nature of the Raman interaction kernel, dynamically shaping the control field to synthesize a tunable coherent filter that selectively addresses specific temporal waveforms. This mechanism enables on-demand storage, filtering, and conversion, providing a coherent interface between MHz- and GHz-bandwidth modes. We validate the platform's selectivity across a basis of 30 orthogonal Hermite-Gaussian modes and certify high-fidelity quantum operation via 5-dimensional process tomography. By combining deterministic mode conversion with bidirectional bandwidth interfacing, we establish the Raman memory as a critical active node for scalable quantum information processing.

摘要翻译

我们提出了一种利用里德堡原子处理器和基于样本的量子对角化方法计算费米-哈伯德模型基态能量的方案。通过利用费米-哈伯德模型与海森堡模型之间的微扰关系，该方案从里德堡原子处理器上制备的海森堡模型中采样，并利用这些样本对大U值条件下的费米-哈伯德模型进行对角化计算。我们引入了各向异性与次近邻相互作用，并探讨了一维费米-哈伯德模型中实现准超导性的相关参数区间。研究展示了在Aquila量子处理器上进行的基态能量与化学势计算的数值与实验结果。我们发现，在研究的参数区间内，海森堡模型采样足以使最多56个量子比特的系统收敛至基态附近，并且即使使用10倍以上样本进行随机采样对比，里德堡原子采样仍显示出明显优势。同时，我们在IBM Quantum硬件上实现了基于门电路的SQD算法对56量子比特哈伯德模型的基准测试。最后，我们通过能隙分析探讨了利用该方法研究涌现超导现象的可行性。

Abstract

We present a method for calculating the ground state energy of the Fermi-Hubbard model leveraging Rydberg atom processors and sample-based quantum diagonalization (SQD). By exploiting the perturbative relationship between the Fermi-Hubbard and Heisenberg models, the procedure samples from the Heisenberg model as prepared on the Rydberg atom processor, and uses the samples to diagonalize the Fermi-Hubbard model for large U. We include anisotropy and next-nearest-neighbor interactions and discuss the relevant regime for quasi-superconductivity in the 1-dimensional Fermi- Hubbard model. Numerical and experimental results on the Aquila quantum processor are presented for ground state energy calculations as well as the chemical potential. We find that the Heisenberg model sampling in the studied regime is sufficient to converge near to the ground state for up to 56 qubits, and we see a clear advantage of Rydberg atom sampling as opposed to random sampling even with 10x more samples for diagonalization. We also present a gate-based implementation of the gate-based SQD algorithm on IBM Quantum hardware for 56-qubit Hubbard model as a benchmark. Finally, we provide a gap analysis for studying emergent superconductivity using this method.

Abstract

Distributed quantum computing can potentially address the scalability challenge by networking processors through photon-mediated remote entanglement. Prior approaches assumed that remote Bell pairs require distillation, resulting in substantial overhead, to achieve sufficiently high fidelity before use. However, recent results show that lattice-surgery operations at logical qubit boundaries tolerate significantly higher error rates than previously assumed. We quantify the resource trade-offs between distillation overhead and surface-code distance requirements under realistic constraints including probabilistic entanglement generation and memory decoherence. We identify the fidelity crossover point separating the two regimes and show that choosing the right strategy can reduce resource overhead by up to two orders of magnitude at low fidelities and up to 68% at high fidelities. We briefly describe the application of these methods to ion-trap and neutral-atom platforms. These results provide co-design principles for optimizing photonic interconnects and fault-tolerant architectures in distributed quantum computers.

Abstract

We propose a hybrid quantum-classical algorithm for the simulation of real-time dynamics in interacting quantum field theories coupled to classical fields, focusing on the self-consistent estimation of semiclassical backreaction. By discretizing space and time, we construct an iterative protocol that simulates the Trotterized dynamics of the quantum fields subject to the dynamical classical fields. By estimating certain quantum expectation values through a set of projective measurements, we source the equations of motion of the classical fields, and solve them numerically to feed them forward to the quantum simulation in an iterative self-consistent loop. Semiclassical backreaction is relevant in various fields of physics, particularly in cosmology, where quantum matter fluctuations affect the gravitational field dynamics, and a controlled renormalization must be carefully considered to get a sensible continuum limit. We benchmark our algorithm in this context, focusing on scalar-tensor theories of modified gravity exhibiting a chameleon mechanism, such that a light classical scalar field driving cosmic acceleration becomes massive in high-density regions, effectively screening any possible yet unobserved fifth force. By focusing on numerically tractable regimes, we explicitly show the convergence and robustness of our algorithm when considering the continuum limit and the effect of quantum shot noise. Our work paves the way for future experiments exploring other non-tractable regimes, including non-perturbative interactions of the quantum fields and how these can change backreaction and the gravitational dynamics.

Abstract

Field emission (FE) electron sources are made close to atomic-scale to reach the highest spatial resolution as well as stable emission for electron microscopy, electron beam inspection and lithography. At present, no single agreed method exists of using FE current-voltage data to extract the apparent emission area, which is needed for predicting some beam properties. The 1956 theory of Murphy and Good (MG) is better physics than the 1920s theory of Fowler and Nordheim (FN) and colleagues, but many researchers use simplified FN theory to analyse experimental data. The present paper reports an experimental method of finding apparent emission area, based on using field ion and field electron microscopes (FIM-FEM). The discrepancy of emission area between the FIM-FEM method and MG-based analysis is a factor of 7.4, while that with simplified FN-based analysis is about 25, confirming MG theory is better for FE data analysis. The result allows deduction of key indicators, including source energy spread, reduced brightness and emission efficiency. A downloadable program is made available to help analysis. Our work provides a new experimental method of characterizing FE electron sources, especially the atomic-scale cold cathode, for which existing plot-based data-analysis methods are not suitable.

Abstract

For continuous-variable Gaussian Markov dynamics, complete positivity couples drift and diffusion at the generator level. For a quantum-limited attenuator with thermal parameter $ν$ and squeezing $r$, the fixed-diffusion Wigner-score (Bayes) reverse drift violates CP iff $\cosh(2r)>ν$. Any Gaussian CP repair must inject extra diffusion, implying $-2\ln F\ge c_{\text{geom}}(ν_{\min})I_{\mathrm{dec}}^{\mathrm{wc}}$.

Abstract

Building on a Guided Quantum Compressor architecture, the approach integrates an autoencoder, a variational quantum circuit, and a classical neural head, and then embeds this hybrid model into a mixture-of-experts framework including a state-of-the-art gradient-boosted tree classifier. Using a European credit card dataset with severe class imbalance, the routed hybrid architecture achieves average precision scores of $0.793\pm0.085$ compared to $0.770\pm0.065$ of XGBoost on 3 repeated 5-fold cross-validation benchmarks. The improvements are achieved while adding only 7 to 21 minutes of extra inference time depending on the choice of hyperparameters. These results indicate that selectively routing transactions to quantum-classical models can enhance fraud detection while remaining compatible with the latency and operational constraints of modern financial institutions.

Score: 0.0 / 14.0
Authors: Ziyi Zhao, Eva Gurra, Michael R. Vissers, K. W. Lehnert

摘要翻译

宽带低损耗超导开关可通过动态重构电路连接性，促进大规模量子信息处理器与低温探测器的发展。这种随时间变化的连接性由无损约瑟夫森结（Josephson junctions）的非线性特性实现，这些结通常被接入超导环路以受磁通量调控。然而，该方法需要耗能的恒定磁通偏置与动态磁通驱动，两者均难以与其他开关或磁通敏感元件隔离，限制了其集成密度。本文设计并表征了一种微波开关，该开关采用持续电流偏置与直流驱动，以降低静态功耗、驱动能耗以及对其他设备的潜在串扰。我们证明，与数十个磁通量子相关的持续电流具有稳定且长寿命的特性，减少了对实时调谐的需求。我们进一步证明，该开关在基于超导电路的量子信息处理中表现出优越性能：其关断模式具有超过20 dB的隔离度，与商用铁氧体隔离器相当；功率处理能力大于100 pW，足以满足谐振器读取信号与放大器泵浦的需求；调制带宽超过600 MHz，适用于多路复用方案。

Abstract

Broadband and low-loss superconducting switches can facilitate large-scale quantum information processors and cryogenic detectors by dynamically reconfiguring the connectivity of their circuits. The time dependent connectivity is enabled by the nonlinearity of lossless Josephson junctions, which are often wired into superconducting loops to be controlled by magnetic flux. However, this approach needs a power-consuming constant flux bias and dynamic flux actuation, both of which are hard to isolate from other switches or flux sensitive elements, limiting their integration density. Here, we design and characterize a microwave switch that implements a persistent current bias and direct current actuation to reduce static power consumption, actuation energy and potential crosstalk to other devices. We show that persistent current associated with tens of flux quanta is stable and long-lived, reducing the need for on-the-fly tuning. We further demonstrate that our switch has desirable performance for superconducting-circuit-based quantum information processing, including an off mode with more than 20 dB isolation comparable to commercial ferrite isolators, power handling larger than 100 pW sufficient for resonator readout tones and amplifier pumps, and modulation bandwidth broader than 600 MHz useful for multiplexing schemes.

72. Completeness for Prime-Dimensional Phase-Affine Circuits FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 14.0
Authors: Colin Blake
Published: 2026-03-06
TL;DR: 该论文将量子比特的CNOT-二面体方程理论推广到素数维量子系统，建立了可逆仿射电路的紧凑PROP表示，通过相位多项式方法推导了统一的传输规则和唯一的相位-仿射规范形式，并证明了语义等价与可推导等价的完备性。
摘要翻译

对电路进行等式推理是量子软件中验证、优化与验证的核心环节。对于量子比特，CNOT-二面体片段通过相位多项式与分层正规形式支持高效重写，形成了一套完备且实际有效的等式理论。本研究将该CNOT-二面体框架从量子比特推广至素数维度的量子比特。我们提出了素数域上可逆仿射电路的紧致PROP，其具有严格对称幺半群语义映射到仿射群，并具备拉丰式仿射正规形式。随后我们引入有限角度对角相位生成元，并依据多项式次数将其组织为线性、二次（奇素数情形）及三次（大于3的素数情形）演算系统。利用二项式基恒等式，我们推导出一致的传输规则，建立了唯一的相位-仿射正规形式，并证明了完备性：语义等价性与可推导等价性相一致。由此获得了一个与相位多项式对齐、适用于素数维度的CNOT-二面体等式理论的广义框架。

Abstract

Equational reasoning about circuits is central in quantum software for validation, optimisation, and verification. For qubits, the CNOT-dihedral fragment supports efficient rewriting via phase polynomials and layered normal forms, yielding a complete and practically effective equational theory. In this work we generalise that CNOT-dihedral picture from qubits to prime-dimensional qudits. We present a compact PROP for reversible affine circuits over a prime field, with a strict symmetric monoidal semantics into the affine group and a Lafont-style affine normal form. We then adjoin finite-angle diagonal phase generators and organise them by polynomial degree, obtaining linear, quadratic (odd prime), and cubic (prime greater than 3) calculi. Using binomial-basis identities we derive uniform transport rules, establish unique phase-affine normal forms, and prove completeness: semantic equality coincides with derivable equality. This yields a prime-dimensional, phase-polynomial-aligned generalisation of the CNOT-dihedral equational theory.

摘要翻译

我们研究了如何从基于半填充哈伯德三脚架（Hubbard tripods）的微观费米子模型中涌现出自旋为1的Affleck-Kennedy-Lieb-Tasaki（AKLT）哈密顿量。首先，我们证明单个三脚架具有一个稳健的三重简并低能流形，对应于一个有效的$S = 1$自由度。该流形在广泛的相互作用范围内占主导地位，并且对中等强度的无序保持稳定。随后，我们结合精确对角化与四阶准简并微扰理论，推导出一对耦合三脚架的有效双线性-双二次自旋模型，并识别出接近目标耦合比的参数区间。特别地，通过调节腿-中心跳跃与两种对称不等价的腿-腿跳跃，我们获得了与双二次-双线性比接近1/3相关的特征性单重态-三重态简并。将分析扩展至三个三脚架，我们比较了不等价的耦合几何构型，并找到了一种策略：在弱耦合区间内，该策略能抑制不必要的长程和多自旋相互作用项，同时保留目标最近邻耦合。这些结果为从哈伯德团簇到可调量子点阵列中的价键固体自旋物理提供了一条具体的自下而上实现路径。

Abstract

We investigate how the spin-1 Affleck-Kennedy-Lieb-Tasaki (AKLT) Hamiltonian can emerge from a microscopic fermionic model based on half-filled Hubbard tripods. We first show that a single tripod hosts a robust threefold-degenerate low-energy manifold corresponding to an effective $S = 1$ degree of freedom. This manifold prevails over a broad range of interactions and remains stable against moderate disorder. We then combine exact diagonalization with fourth-order quasi-degenerate perturbation theory to derive an effective bilinear-biquadratic spin model for a pair of coupled tripods and identify coupling regimes where the target ratio is approached. In particular, tuning leg-center hopping together with two symmetry-inequivalent leg-leg hoppings yields the characteristic singlet-triplet degeneracy associated with a biquadratic-to-bilinear ratio close to 1/3. Extending the analysis to three tripods, we compare nonequivalent coupling geometries and find a strategy that suppresses unwanted longer-range and multispin terms while preserving the target nearest-neighbor couplings in the weak-coupling regime. These results establish a concrete bottom-up route from Hubbard clusters to valence-bond-solid spin physics in tunable quantum-dot arrays.

Authors: Chen-Yu Liu, Leonardo Placidi, Eric Brunner, Enrico Rinaldi

摘要翻译

我们提出一种相关性-复杂度映射图，作为实用诊断工具，用于判断现实世界数据分布是否在结构上与IQP型量子生成模型相匹配。该工具通过两个互补指标进行表征：（i）量子相关性相似度指标，通过数据集的关联阶（沃尔什-哈达玛/傅里叶）功率谱按相互作用阶聚合计算，并采用詹森-香农散度相对于独立同分布二项参考分布进行量化；（ii）经典相关性-复杂度指标，定义为最优Chow-Liu树近似无法捕捉的总相关性比例，并以总相关性进行归一化。我们通过将量子相关性相似度指标与支撑集失配机制关联提供理论支持：对于采用最大均值差异目标函数训练的固定架构IQP族，更高的量子相关性相似度指标意味着更小的不可约近似下限。利用该映射图，我们识别出经典湍流数据同时具备IQP兼容性与经典复杂性（高量子相关性相似度指标/高经典相关性-复杂度指标）。在此定位指导下，我们采用可逆浮点-比特串表示与潜参数自适应方案，通过学习并插值低维潜轨迹，在时间序列上复用紧凑型IQP电路。在与受限玻尔兹曼机、深度卷积生成对抗网络等经典模型的对比评估中，IQP方法在显著减少训练快照数量并使用小型潜模块的条件下，实现了具有竞争力的分布对齐效果，这支持了将量子相关性相似度指标/经典相关性-复杂度指标作为定位IQP适配领域、推进量子生成效用的实用指标。

Abstract

We propose a Correlation-Complexity Map as a practical diagnostic tool for determining when real-world data distributions are structurally aligned with IQP-type quantum generative models. Characterized by two complementary indicators: (i) a Quantum Correlation-Likeness Indicator (QCLI), computed from the dataset's correlation-order (Walsh-Hadamard/Fourier) power spectrum aggregated by interaction order and quantified via Jensen-Shannon divergence from an i.i.d. binomial reference; and (ii) a Classical Correlation-Complexity Indicator (CCI), defined as the fraction of total correlation not captured by the optimal Chow-Liu tree approximation, normalized by total correlation. We provide theoretical support by relating QCLI to a support-mismatch mechanism, for fixed-architecture IQP families trained with an MMD objective, higher QCLI implies a smaller irreducible approximation floor. Using the map, we identify the classical turbulence data as both IQP-compatible and classically complex (high QCLI/high CCI). Guided by this placement, we use an invertible float-to-bitstring representation and a latent-parameter adaptation scheme that reuses a compact IQP circuit over a temporal sequence by learning and interpolating a low-dimensional latent trajectory. In comparative evaluations against classical models such as Restricted Boltzmann Machine (RBM) and Deep Convolutional Generative Adversarial Networks (DCGAN), the IQP approach achieves competitive distributional alignment while using substantially fewer training snapshots and a small latent block, supporting the use of QCLI/CCI as practical indicators for locating IQP-aligned domains and advancing generative quantum utility.

75. Entanglement distribution: To herald or not to herald FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 14.0
Authors: Jeffrey H. Shapiro, Clark Embleton, J. Gabriel Richardson
Published: 2026-03-06
TL;DR: 该论文比较了三种基于光谱岛的量子纠缠分发系统（两种使用预示，一种不使用）的纠缠分发速率，发现对于90%或更低的预示效率，零附加损耗复用系统的速率超过信号路径擦除系统，但两者都低于非预示操作，同时这些性能差异需要权衡不同系统的设备要求。
摘要翻译

高速率、高保真度的纠缠分发对于构建量子互联网至关重要，而目前自发参量下转换器（SPDC）是向Alice和Bob量子节点传输纠缠信号-闲置光子对的首选源。在这方面，基于相位匹配频谱岛的SPDC尤其具有吸引力，因为它们能提供具有单模时间行为的波分复用信号-闲置光子对。本文比较了三种基于频谱岛系统的纠缠分发速率。其中两种系统利用闲置光子探测进行预示：基于频谱岛的无附加损耗复用（ZALM）系统，以及采用信号路径擦除的基于频谱岛萨格纳克SPDC源。第三种系统则采用非预示型萨格纳克SPDC源。在预示效率为90%或更低的情况下，ZALM的每泵浦脉冲纠缠分发速率超过信号路径擦除源，且当三个系统均使用$N_I$个频谱岛并为每个泵浦脉冲分配$N_M = N_I$个量子存储器时，这两种速率均低于非预示型操作。然而，这些性能表现必须结合三个系统不同的设备需求进行权衡：例如，ZALM需要一对完美匹配的萨格纳克源，这是信号路径擦除方案无需承担的显著负担；此外，若两种预示系统无法实现高预示效率，其性能相较于非预示型操作将处于劣势。

Abstract

High-rate, high-fidelity entanglement distribution is essential for the creation of a quantum internet, and spontaneous parametric downconverters (SPDCs) are, at present, the preferred sources of entangled signal-idler photon pairs for transmission to Alice and Bob's quantum nodes. SPDCs using phase-matched spectral islands are especially attractive, in this regard, because they provide wavelength-division multiplexed signal-idler pairs with single-mode temporal behavior. This paper compares the entanglement distribution rates of three islands-based systems. Two use idler detections for heralding: islands-based zero-added-loss multiplexing (ZALM), and an islands-based Sagnac SPDC source with signal-path erasure. The third employs an unheralded Sagnac SPDC source. For 90% or lower heralding efficiencies, ZALM's per-pump-pulse entanglement distribution rate exceeds that of the signal-path erasure source, and both rates are inferior to unheralded operation's when all three systems employ $N_I$ spectral islands and allocate $N_M = N_I$ quantum memories to each pump pulse. These behaviors, however, must be weighed against the three systems' differing equipment requirements, e.g., ZALM requires a pair of perfectly-matched Sagnac sources, which is a significant burden not incurred by the signal-path erasure approach, and both heralded systems will suffer, in comparison with unheralded operation, if they cannot realize high heralding efficiencies.

77. Entanglement is not sufficient for most practical entanglement-based QKD protocols FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 14.0
Authors: Shubhayan Sarkar, Tushita Prasad, Karol Horodecki
Published: 2026-03-06
TL;DR: 该论文研究发现，在存在经典侧信息泄漏的情况下，纠缠态对于标准的实用纠缠基量子密钥分发协议（如E91或纠缠基BB84协议）并不足够，并识别了一类在各向同性态下无法提取安全密钥的纠缠态，同时为基于中继器的QKD架构的可扩展性提供了上界分析工具。
摘要翻译

量子密钥分发（QKD）是量子信息理论中探索最为深入的应用之一。基于纠缠的QKD（EB-QKD）中的一个核心问题是：是否所有纠缠态都能用于提取密钥？我们观察到，在标准的实用EB-QKD协议（例如E91协议或基于纠缠的BB84类协议）中，当存在任意微小的经典侧信息泄露时，纠缠并不足以保证密钥提取——即使协议中希望共享安全密钥的参与方会公开其输入选择。我们通过识别一类两量子比特各向同性态来证明这一点：这些态虽然处于纠缠状态，但在上述协议中，无论参与方进行何种测量，都无法用于提取密钥。反直觉的是，即使泄露仅来自协议的“无效轮次”（即无法用于生成密钥的轮次），这种差距依然存在。随后，我们将这一结果推广到任意维度和任意参与方数量，通过识别一类各向同性态表明：即使它们处于纠缠状态，在此类协议下也无法用于提取安全密钥。最后，我们证明，我们的方法提供了一种工具，能够以与协议无关的方式对基于中继器的QKD架构的可扩展性给出上界。有趣的是，我们发现，即使在制备过程中允许存在极微小的噪声，也会大幅降低QKD网络的可扩展性。

Abstract

Quantum key distribution (QKD) is the most explored application of quantum information theory. A central problem in entanglement-based QKD (EB-QKD), is whether every entangled state can be used to extract a key. We observe that entanglement is not sufficient for standard practical EB-QKD protocols where the input choices are announced by the parties that want to share a secure key, such as E91 or entanglement-based BB84 type protocols, when even an arbitrarily small amount of leakage of classical side information occurs. We do this by identifying a class of two-qubit isotropic states that are entangled but cannot be used to distil the key under such protocols for any possible measurement by the parties. Counter-intuitively, this gap persists even when the leakage occurs from the "junk" rounds of the protocol, i.e, rounds that cannot be used to generate any key. We then extend this result to arbitrary dimensions and parties by identifying a class of isotropic states that are not useful to extract a secure key under such protocols, even if they are entangled. Finally, we demonstrate that our approach provides a tool to upper-bound the scalability of repeater-based QKD architectures in a protocol-independent manner. Interestingly, we find that allowing for even a tiny noise in the preparation drastically reduces the scalability of the QKD network.

摘要翻译

本文提出了一种包含分子内部核动力学的分子间库仑电子俘获（ICEC）分析模型。在ICEC过程中，一个电子通过将多余能量转移给邻近原子或分子并使其电离，从而附着到另一个原子或分子上。尽管先前的理论研究假设原子核固定，但近期研究表明，两个ICEC参与体之间的相对运动对该过程有显著影响。在此，我们将相关分子的内部核运动纳入ICEC截面的分析方程中。我们采用两种方法：1. 利用理论振动分辨光电离截面；2. 应用弗兰克-康登原理。我们的理论可推导出电子能谱、单个振动跃迁的ICEC截面以及温度依赖的截面。核动力学导致电子截面分布在多个振动态上，并在我们的模型系统H+ LiH中，触发了ICEC过程中LiH的解离。

Abstract

We present an analytical model for intermolecular Coulombic electron capture (ICEC) which includes the internal nuclear dynamics of the molecules involved. In ICEC, an electron attaches to an atom or molecule by transferring excess energy to a neighbor, ionizing said neighbor. While previous theoretical investigations assumed fixed nuclei, recent studies indicate that relative motion between the two ICEC partners significantly influences the process. Here, we incorporate the internal nuclear motion of the molecules involved into an analytical equation of the ICEC cross section. We employ two approaches: 1. utilizing theoretical vibrationally resolved photoionization cross sections and 2. applying the Franck-Condon principle. Our theory yields electron spectra, ICEC cross sections for individual vibronic transitions, and temperature dependent cross sections. Nuclear dynamics lead to a distribution of the electronic cross section over several vibrational states and, in our model system H+ LiH, triggers dissociation of LiH during ICEC.

Abstract

We introduce an $\varepsilon$-approximate unitary 2-design that is compatible with the structure of p- and q-quadratures in continuous-variable (CV) quantum systems. The design unitaries are defined on a finite-dimensional discretisation of the CV space and can be physically implemented as operations on the full CV space. This establishes the first approximate unitary design for CV systems. The design alternatingly acts with unitaries based on the quadrature operators $\hat q$ and $\hat p$. We prove that the parameter $\varepsilon$ is given by $1/d^\ell$, where $d$ is the dimension of the truncated Hilbert space and $\ell$ is the number of iterations. We propose an Unclonable Encryption scheme in which the encryption operators are given by the unitaries which constitute the approximate unitary design. We prove its security using recent results on decoupling. This establishes unclonable-indistinguishable security for a CV encryption for the first time.

Authors: Anthony Micciche, Naphan Benchasattabuse, Andrew McGregor, Michal Hajdušek, Rodney Van Meter, Stefan Krastanov

Abstract

We investigate the problem of compiling the generation of graph states to arbitrarily many distributed homogeneous quantum processing units (QPUs), providing a scalable partitioning algorithm and graph state generation protocol to minimize the number of Bell pairs required. To this goal, we consider the problem of balanced k graph partitioning with the objective of minimizing the sizes of the maximum matchings between partitions, a more natural measure of entanglement compared to the naive but common metric of cut edges. We show that our heuristic algorithm, BURY, partitions graph states to require fewer Bell pairs for generation than state-of-the-art k partition algorithms. Furthermore, we show that BURY reduces the cut-rank of the partitions, demonstrating that the partitioning found by our algorithm is likely to minimize the Bell pair utilization of any future improved distributed graph state generation protocol. Additionally, we discuss how one could straightforwardly apply our methods to the dynamic case where the graph state generation and measurement are performed concurrently. Our study of the balanced minimum maximum matching k partition problem and the heuristic algorithm we design provides a scalable foundation for reducing quantum network overhead for distributed measurement-based quantum computation (MBQC), as well as any scheme where distributed graph state generation is desired.

81. Unifying Graph Measures and Stabilizer Decompositions for the Classical Simulation of Quantum Circuits FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 14.0
Authors: Julien Codsi, Tuomas Laakkonen
Published: 2026-03-06
TL;DR: 该论文提出了一个统一框架，将量子电路经典模拟的稳定子分解和张量网络收缩方法结合起来，并基于此开发了两种具有改进时间复杂度的新算法，同时引入了更高效的聚焦树宽和聚焦秩宽复杂度度量。
摘要翻译

为在经典硬件上模拟量子电路，已发展出多种算法。其中最突出的方法基于**稳定子分解**（stabilizer decompositions）与**张量网络收缩**（tensor network contraction）。本文提出一个统一框架，将这两种方法置于共同的形式体系下，从而建立起二者间的桥梁。基于此框架，我们提出了两种模拟 $n$ 量子比特电路 $C$ 的新算法：一种运行时间为 $\tilde{O}(T^{\mathsf{tw}(C)})$，另一种为 $\tilde{O}(T^{γ\cdot \mathsf{rw}(C)})$，其中 $\mathsf{tw}(C)$ 和 $\mathsf{rw}(C)$ 分别表示与 $C$ 关联的张量网络的树宽（tree-width）和秩宽（rank-width），$T$ 为 $C$ 中非克利福德门（non-Clifford gates）的数量，且 $γ\approx 3.42$。所提出的算法结构简洁，仅需线性内存，易于并行化，并能与 ZX 图（ZX-diagram）简化流程良好结合。此外，我们引入了精细化的复杂度度量——**聚焦树宽**（focused tree-width）与**聚焦秩宽**（focused rank-width），其效率始终不低于对应的标准度量；这些度量可直接应用于我们的模拟算法中，从而为运行时间提供更精确的上界估计。

Abstract

Various algorithms have been developed to simulate quantum circuits on classical hardware. Among the most prominent are approaches based on \emph{stabilizer decompositions} and \emph{tensor network contraction}. In this work, we present a unified framework that bridges these two approaches, placing them under a common formalism. Using this, we present two new algorithms to simulate an $n$-qubit circuit $C$: one that runs in $\tilde{O}(T^{\mathsf{tw}(C)})$ time and the other in $\tilde{O}(T^{γ\cdot \mathsf{tw}(C)})$ time, where $\mathsf{tw}(C)$ and $\mathsf{rw}(C)$ refer to the the tree-width and rank-width, respectively, of a tensor network associated to $C$, $T$ is the number of non-Clifford gates in $C$, and $γ\approx 3.42$. The proposed algorithms are simple, only require a linear amount of memory, are trivially parallelizable, and interact nicely with ZX-diagram simplification routines. Furthermore, we introduce the refined complexity measures \emph{focused tree-width} and \emph{focused rank-width}, which are always at least as efficient as their standard equivalent; these can be directly applied within our simulation algorithms, allowing for a more precise upper bound on the run time.

Abstract

We improve the accuracy of Active Volume resource estimates by explicitly scheduling when Active Volume blocks execute. 84. Universal Dynamical Scaling of Strong-to-Weak Spontaneous Symmetry Breaking in Open Quantum Systems FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 14.0
Authors: Chang Shu, Kai Zhang, Kai Sun
Published: 2026-03-06
TL;DR: 该论文研究了开放量子系统中强到弱自发对称破缺（SWSSB）的普适动力学标度行为，发现对称性（而非谱隙结构）控制着SWSSB的晚期动力学标度，为开放量子系统中的非平衡对称破缺提供了新途径。
摘要翻译

强至弱自发对称破缺（Strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry breaking，简称SWSSB）定义了一种不存在纯态对应物的混合物质态相，其中诸如Rényi-2关联子之类的非线性可观测量会发展出长程有序，而传统的线性关联则保持短程性。本文研究了一维开放量子系统中由Lindblad演化支配的SWSSB涌现现象，其中转变时间随系统尺寸发散，且SWSSB仅在稳态中渐近地出现。通过追踪Rényi-2关联长度的晚期增长，我们发现了一个完全由Lindblad算符的对称性类别所控制的普适动力学区域。与通常认为晚期动力学由Liouvillian谱的低能部分主导的预期相反，我们发现SWSSB转变的时间依赖性——指数型或代数型——完全由对称性决定，而与Lindblad算符的细节无关，包括Liouvillian谱是否具有能隙。对于具有$\mathbb{Z}_2$对称性的动力学，Rényi-2关联长度随时间呈指数增长——即使谱是无能隙的——从而产生有效的转变时间$t_c \propto \operatorname{ln} L$，并使得$\mathbb{Z}_2$ SWSSB稳态能够被快速制备。相比之下，具有U(1)对称性的动力学则表现出代数标度行为$t_c \propto L^α$，其动力学指数依赖于粒子填充数：有限填充下的弹道增长（$α\approx 1$）在零填充极限下过渡到扩散标度（$α= 2$）。这些结果表明，对称性——而非能隙结构——是控制SWSSB晚期动力学标度的主导原则，并为开放量子系统中的非平衡对称性破缺开辟了一条新路径。

Abstract

Strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry breaking (SWSSB) defines a mixed-state phase of matter--without a pure-state counterpart--in which nonlinear observables such as the Rényi-2 correlator develop long-range order while conventional linear correlations remain short-ranged. Here we study the emergence of SWSSB in one-dimensional open quantum systems governed by Lindbladian evolution, where the transition time diverges with system size and SWSSB appears only asymptotically in the steady state. By tracking the late-time growth of the Rényi-2 correlation length, we uncover a universal dynamical regime controlled purely by the symmetry class of the Lindbladian. Contrary to the conventional expectation that late-time dynamics are governed by the low-lying Liouvillian spectrum, we find that the time dependence of the SWSSB transition--exponential versus algebraic--is dictated solely by symmetry, independent of details of the Lindbladian, including whether the Liouvillian spectrum is gapped or gapless. For $\mathbb{Z}_2$-symmetric dynamics, the Rényi-2 correlation length grows exponentially in time--even when the spectrum is gapless--yielding an effective transition time $t_c \propto \operatorname{ln} L$ and enabling rapid preparation of the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ SWSSB steady state. In contrast, U(1)-symmetric dynamics exhibit algebraic scaling, $t_c \propto L^α$, with a filling-dependent dynamical exponent: ballistic growth ($α\approx 1$) at finite filling crosses over to diffusive scaling ($α= 2$) in the zero-filling limit. These results establish symmetry--rather than spectral gap structure--as the controlling principle for SWSSB late-time dynamical scaling, and open a new route to nonequilibrium symmetry breaking in open quantum systems.

TL;DR: 该研究探索了量子计算在模拟云滴碰撞-聚并过程中的应用，提出了一种基于主方程的量子算法，相比经典方法实现了指数级效率提升。
摘要翻译

量子计算作为一种解决诸多科学领域复杂问题的新兴途径正受到广泛关注。在大气与海洋科学中，它可能有助于降低模拟大规模非线性系统的计算成本。然而，量子计算机在该领域的应用研究仍处于早期阶段，尚未确立合适的应用场景。本研究探索了利用量子计算模拟云滴碰撞-并合过程的方法，该过程主导着云微物理中液态粒子的尺度增长。受金融工程领域已开发的量子算法启发，我们提出了一种基于主方程的新算法，该方程描述了云滴质量分布的时间演化。我们的算法利用量子振幅编码云滴质量分布的概率，并通过量子振幅估计计算云滴的预期数量。资源分析表明，T门数量按$O(N^2)$比例缩放，其中$N$为质量分布的区间数量。相较于经典方法仅能随$N$呈指数级增长，这构成了本质性改进。该效率提升是通过在叠加态中使用量子算术，以及编码跃迁历史而非每个时间步的完整分布实现的。我们的研究结果表明，碰撞-并合过程是大气科学领域中具有潜力的量子计算应用目标之一。

Abstract

Quantum computing is gaining attention as a new approach for solving complex problems in many scientific fields. In atmospheric and oceanic sciences, it may help reduce computational costs of simulating large and nonlinear systems. However, research into the use of quantum computers in this area is still in its earlier stage, and suitable applications have not been established yet. This study explores the use of quantum computing for calculating the collision-coalescence process of cloud droplets, which dominates the size growth of liquid particles in the cloud microphysics. Inspired by the quantum algorithms developed in the field of financial engineering, we propose a new algorithm based on a master equation that describes the time evolution of the droplet mass distribution. Our algorithm uses the quantum amplitudes to encode the probability distribution of droplet mass and calculates the expected number of droplets via the quantum amplitude estimation. Our resource analysis shows that the number of T gates scales as $O(N^2)$, where $N$ is the number of bins of the mass distributions. This is an essential improvement over the classical methods that scale only exponentially with $N$. This efficiency improvement is achieved by using quantum arithmetic in the superposition and by encoding the transition histories instead of the full distributions at each time step. Our results suggest that the collision-coalescence process is one of the promising targets of quantum computing in the field of atmospheric science.

86. Efficient Classical Simulation of Low-Rank-Width Quantum Circuits Using ZX-Calculus FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 14.0
Authors: Fedor Kuyanov, Aleks Kissinger
Published: 2026-03-06
TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于ZX演算和秩宽度参数的高效经典模拟量子电路的方法，显著减少了浮点运算量。
摘要翻译

本文提出了一种基于秩宽收缩（即数值计算）ZX图的技术，该技术的计算复杂度与图的秩宽参数相关，而该参数在ZX图重写规则下具有良好的性质。给定宽度为$R$的秩分解，我们的方法能以$Õ(4^R)$时间复杂度模拟类图式ZX图。应用于量子电路的经典模拟时，该方法的速度不亚于朴素态矢量模拟或稳定子分解（设$α=0.5$），在实际应用中若采用适当选取的秩分解，其速度可显著提升。由于寻找最优秩分解属于NP难问题，我们提出了在实践中能生成高质量分解的启发式算法。通过将我们的模拟程序与主流张量收缩库Quimb进行基准测试，我们观察到对于随机及结构化非克利福德电路，以及随机ZX图，浮点运算量均大幅减少（通常可达数个数量级）。

Abstract

In this paper, we introduce a technique for contracting (i.e. numerically evaluating) ZX-diagrams whose complexity scales with their rank-width, a graph parameter that behaves nicely under ZX rewrite rules. Given a rank-decomposition of width $R$, our method simulates a graph-like ZX-diagram in $Õ(4^R)$ time. Applied to classical simulation of quantum circuits, it is no slower than either naive state vector simulation or stabiliser decompositions with $α= 0.5$, and in practice can be significantly faster for suitably chosen rank-decompositions. Since finding optimal rank-decompositions is NP-hard, we introduce heuristics that produce good decompositions in practice. We benchmark our simulation routine against Quimb, a popular tensor contraction library, and observe substantial reductions in floating-point operations (often by several orders of magnitude) for random and structured non-Clifford circuits as well as random ZX-diagrams.

87. Thermodynamics of Quantum Coupled Transport FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 14.0
Authors: Shuvadip Ghosh, Arnab Ghosh
Published: 2026-03-06
TL;DR: 该论文研究了纳米尺度量子系统中耦合输运过程的热力学行为，通过熵产生率框架分析了量子点系统中的能量与粒子耦合输运，揭示了热电效应等热力学交叉效应的产生机制以及逆电流现象的实现条件。
摘要翻译

本综述从热力学视角探讨纳米尺度系统中的量子耦合输运过程。我们的分析基于熵产率框架展开，该核心物理量主导非平衡过程，并通过共轭力-流对进行表述。尽管热力学定律在经典与量子领域具有普适性，本文的讨论将在微观开放量子系统框架下展开，重点关注与电子库耦合的量子点（QDs）体系。我们首先考察基本的单输运过程，并强调其在近平衡区域所受的强热力学约束。这引出了对耦合输运的研究——在该过程中多个力-流对共存并相互作用，从而产生更丰富的热力学行为。以熵产率为指导原则，我们分析了最小化双端单量子点结构中的耦合能量与粒子输运，并阐明传统热电现象（包括塞贝克效应、帕尔帖效应以及热电热机与制冷机）如何自然地作为热力学交叉效应呈现。随后，我们将该框架拓展至三端耦合量子点（CQD）构型，该构型为研究耦合输运提供了多功能平台，并在适当约束下可简化为著名的Sánchez-Büttiker构型。除标准交叉效应外，我们进一步探讨耦合输运中的逆流现象（ICC），即电流在互平行的热力学力驱动下反向流动而不违反第二定律。我们证明ICC的实现需要打破能量与粒子输运之间的对称性，并明确了在具有吸引性点间相互作用的耦合量子点系统中实现该现象的条件。

Abstract

This review presents a thermodynamic perspective on quantum coupled transport processes in nanoscale systems. Our analysis is formulated within the framework of entropy production rate, the central quantity governing non-equilibrium processes and expressed through conjugate force-flux pairs. Although thermodynamic laws are universal across classical and quantum domains, the discussion is developed within a microscopic open quantum system framework, focusing on quantum dots (QDs) coupled to electronic reservoirs. We first examine elementary single transport processes and highlight their strong thermodynamic constraints in the near-equilibrium regime. This motivates the study of coupled transport, where multiple force-flux pairs coexist and interact, leading to richer thermodynamic behaviour. Using entropy production as the guiding principle, we analyse coupled energy and particle transport in a minimal two-terminal single-QD setup and show how conventional thermoelectric phenomena, including Seebeck and Peltier effects as well as thermoelectric heat engines and refrigerators, naturally emerge as thermodynamic cross-effects. We then extend the framework to a three-terminal coupled quantum dot (CQD) geometry, which provides a versatile platform for studying coupled transport and reduces, under suitable constraints, to the well-known Sánchez-Büttiker configuration. Beyond standard cross-effects, we discuss the phenomenon of inverse currents in coupled transport (ICC), where a current flows against mutually parallel thermodynamic forces without violating the second law. We show that ICC requires breaking the symmetry between energy and particle transport and identify the conditions for its realization in coupled quantum-dot systems with attractive interdot interactions.

Authors: George Pennington, Kevin C. Smith, James R. Garrison, Lachlan P. Lindoy, Jason Crain, Ben Jaderberg

摘要翻译

对称保护拓扑（SPT）相拓展了量子物质的朗道范式，它允许存在缺乏任何局域序参量却仍保持对称性的不同物相。在可编程量子处理器上大规模演示这些物相，是利用量子硬件探测涌现多体现象的关键里程碑，但这一目标通常受限于捕获非平凡纠缠所需的电路深度。本文采用基于张量网络的近似量子编译（AQC）协议，构建了浅层量子电路（18-39层CNOT门深度），以97.9%-99.0%的保真度制备了自旋-1/2键交替海森堡链在两种SPT相中的100位点基态。在IBM量子硬件上执行这些电路后，所得态展现出SPT序的所有定义性特征：包括长度达20的非局域弦序、纠缠谱中的特征简并，以及对称保护边缘模的明确证据。这些独立诊断特征的同时观测，确立了当前量子计算机作为研究对称保护量子物质的大规模通用平台的地位。更广泛而言，我们的研究为在经典计算方法难以处理的区域中探测此类系统的非平衡淬火动力学奠定了实践基础。

Abstract

Symmetry-protected topological (SPT) phases extend the Landau paradigm of quantum matter by admitting distinct symmetry-preserving phases that lack any local order parameter. Demonstrating these phases at scale on programmable quantum processors is a key milestone in using quantum hardware to probe emergent many-body phenomena, yet it is impeded by the circuit depth normally required to capture non-trivial entanglement. Here we use a tensor network based approximate quantum compiling (AQC) protocol to construct shallow quantum circuits (18-39 CNOT depth), which prepare 100-site ground states of the spin-1/2 bond-alternating Heisenberg chain in both SPT phases, to 97.9-99.0% fidelity. Upon executing the circuits on IBM quantum hardware, the resulting states exhibit all defining signatures of SPT order including non-local string order for strings of up to length 20, characteristic degeneracies in the entanglement spectrum and clear evidence of symmetry-protected edge modes. The simultaneous observation of these independent diagnostics establishes current quantum computers as versatile platforms for large-scale studies of symmetry-protected quantum matter. More broadly, our results establish a practical foundation for probing non-equilibrium quench dynamics of such systems in regimes that challenge classical computational methods.

89. Leakage-protected idle operation of a triangular exchange-only spin qubit FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 14.0
Authors: Joseph D. Broz, Jesse C. Hoke, Edwin Acuna, Jason R. Petta
Published: 2026-03-06
TL;DR: 该论文研究了三角形交换自旋量子比特在泄漏保护空闲点下的相干性，通过精确控制交换耦合实现了对计算子空间泄漏的抑制，并测量了退相干时间，发现其性能在特定条件下优于传统交换自旋量子比特。
摘要翻译

我们表征了在泄漏保护空闲点（LPI）下工作的三角交换唯自旋量子比特的相干性。三角几何结构允许独立控制所有三对交换相互作用，而当这些耦合同时开启并调至等强度时，即满足LPI条件。在此配置下，交换相互作用会诱导一个能隙 $E_g = 3J/2$，该能隙可抑制计算子空间中的泄漏，同时保持量子比特状态不受影响。我们开发了校准LPI点和测量 $E_g$ 的流程，并利用这些流程在宽范围的能隙能量下表征量子比特的退相干时间。尽管在持续开启大交换耦合的条件下工作会使量子比特暴露于电荷噪声，但我们发现，当 $E_g/h < 60$ MHz 时，其 $\tilde{T}_2^*$ 仍超过传统交换唯自旋量子比特。本文展示的对同时性、全连接交换的精确控制，为提升交换唯自旋量子比特的性能提供了一条自然路径，同时也为实现新型量子比特编码提供了可能。

Abstract

We characterize the coherence of a triangular exchange-only (EO) spin qubit operated at a leakage-protected idle (LPI) point. The triangular geometry enables independent control of all three pairwise exchange interactions, and the LPI condition occurs when these couplings are turned on simultaneously and tuned to equal strength. In this configuration, the exchange interaction induces an energy gap $E_g = 3J/2$ that suppresses leakage from the computational subspace while leaving the qubit state unaffected. We develop procedures to calibrate the LPI point and measure $E_g$, and use these to characterize the qubit dephasing time over a broad range of gap energies. While operating with large always-on exchange couplings exposes the qubit to charge noise, we find that $\tilde{T}_2^*$ still exceeds that of conventional exchange-only spin qubits for $E_g/h < 60$ MHz. The precise control of simultaneous, all-to-all connected exchange demonstrated here presents a natural path towards improving the performance of EO qubits and also enables novel qubit encodings.

Authors: Martina Jung, Suchitra Krishnaswamy, Timon Schapeler, Annabelle Bohrdt, Tim J. Bartley, Jan Sperling, Martin Gärttner

摘要翻译

非经典性（在量子光学意义上定义）是光子量子技术的资源。因此，认证量子态的非经典性对于评估其实现量子优势的潜力至关重要。然而，传统非经典性见证方法通常假设对可观测量具有完美认知，在统计有限且光子探测器分辨率受限的实际场景中往往失效。此外，这些见证方法未能利用以下事实：在特定实验中，某些量子态出现的可能性极低。本文中，我们训练了一个变分模型，利用多模量子态在多种光子数分辨探测方案下获得的有限测量样本，来区分经典态与非经典态。所学习到的决策规则即为非经典性的指示器，并针对给定的一组物理相关态进行定制。我们的方法既是数据驱动的，又具有可解释性——因为可以提取出学习得到的解析决策规则。通过使用（i）超导纳米线单光子探测器与（ii）时间复用探测方案测量的实验数据对模型进行训练，验证了该方法的通用性，为高效的非经典性检测开辟了新途径。

Abstract

Nonclassicality, defined in the quantum optical sense, serves as a resource for photon-based quantum technologies. Therefore, certifying the nonclassicality of a quantum state is crucial for gauging its potential for quantum advantage. However, traditional nonclassicality witnesses that assume perfect knowledge of the witness observables often fail in realistic scenarios with limited statistics and finite-resolution photon detectors. Furthermore, these witnesses do not exploit the fact that certain states are unlikely to be observed in a given experiment. Here, we train a variational model to distinguish classical from nonclassical states using finitely many measurement samples of multimode quantum states that are probed with different photon-number-resolving detection schemes. The learned decision rule is then an indicator of nonclassicality, tailored to a given set of physically relevant states. Our approach is both data-driven and interpretable in the sense that the learned analytical decision rule can be extracted. Training the model on experimental data measured with (i) a superconducting nanowire single-photon detector and (ii) a time-bin multiplexing detection scheme demonstrates the versatility of the approach, paving the way for efficient nonclassicality detection.

91. The stabilizer ground state and applications to quantum simulation FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 14.0
Authors: Yuping Mao, Chang Chen, Jiaxing Feng, Yimeng Mao, Tim Byrnes
Published: 2026-03-06
TL;DR: 该论文定义了最优稳定子基态，提出了一种通过遗传算法和稳定子表格形式高效逼近真实基态的方法，并应用于基于测量的确定性虚时演化量子模拟。
摘要翻译

稳定子基态被定义为相对于给定哈密顿量能量最低的稳定子态。在许多情况下，该态高度简并，并不给出唯一的稳定子态。我们将最优稳定子基态定义为与真实基态保真度最高的稳定子基态。这在量子模拟背景下非常有用，因为它允许通过克利福德电路近似一个基态，并可进一步优化以逼近真实基态。我们展示了如何计算最优稳定子基态。我们进一步展示了该态在基于测量的确定性虚时间演化（MITE）中的应用，该方法能以高效率收敛至基态。通过经典地选择最优稳定子生成元组并采用稳定子表格形式体系，该方法可制备出具有最大保真度的对应稳定子基态。该生成元组的识别与优化是通过针对目标哈密顿量结构定制的遗传算法实现的。复杂度分析进一步表明，该算法的量子资源成本随系统规模呈多项式增长，凸显了其高效性及潜在的量子优势。

Abstract

The stabilizer ground state is defined is the lowest energy stabilizer state with respect to a given Hamiltonian. In many cases it is highly degenerate and does not give a unique stabilizer state. We define the optimal stabilizer ground state as the stabilizer ground state which has the highest fidelity with the true ground state. This is useful in quantum simulation contexts as it allows for a Clifford circuit approximation of a ground state that can be further refined towards the true ground state. We show how the optimal stabilizer ground state may be evaluated. We show applications of this state in the context of measurement-based deterministic imaginary time evolution (MITE), which converges to the ground state with high efficiency. By classically selecting the optimal stabilizer generator group and employing the stabilizer tableaux formalism, the method prepares the corresponding stabilizer ground state with maximal fidelity. The identification and refinement of this generator group are performed using a genetic algorithm tailored to the structure of the target Hamiltonian. The complexity analysis further demonstrates that algorithm's quantum resource cost scales polynomially with system size, highlighting its high efficiency and potential quantum advantage.

Abstract

We propose a quantum implicit neural representation (QINR)-based autoencoder (AE) and variational autoencoder (VAE) for image reconstruction and generation tasks. Our purpose is to demonstrate that the QINR in VAEs and AEs can transform information from the latent space into highly rich, periodic, and high-frequency features. Additionally, we aim to show that the QINR-VAE can be more stable than various quantum generative adversarial network (QGAN) models in image generation because it can address the low diversity problem. Our quantum-classical hybrid models consist of a classical convolutional neural network (CNN) encoder and a quantum-based QINR decoder. We train the QINR-AE/VAE with binary cross-entropy with logits (BCEWithLogits) as the reconstruction loss. For the QINR-VAE, we additionally employ Kullback-Leibler divergence for latent regularization with beta/capacity scheduling to prevent posterior collapse. We introduce learnable angle-scaling in data reuploading to address optimization challenges. We test our models on the MNIST, E-MNIST, and Fashion-MNIST datasets to reconstruct and generate images. Our results demonstrate that the QINR structure in VAE can produce a wider variety of images with a small amount of data than various generative models that have been studied. We observe that the generated and reconstructed images from the QINR-VAE/AE are clear with sharp boundaries and details. Overall, we find that the addition of QINR-based quantum layers into the AE/VAE frameworks enhances the performance of reconstruction and generation with a constrained set of parameters.

93. Unified and computable approach to optimal strategies for multiparameter estimation FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 14.0
Authors: Zhao-Yi Zhou, Da-Jian Zhang
Published: 2026-03-06

摘要翻译

物理参数的精确估计是科学发现与技术发展的基石。量子计量学与传感的核心目标在于利用纠缠等量子资源，设计出尽可能精确估计物理参数的最优策略。尽管单参数量子计量已取得显著进展，但由于参数不兼容性问题，多参数场景的挑战性依然显著更高。本研究提出了一种统一且可计算的方法，用于同时估计多个参数，并达到量子力学所允许的最终精度。该方法的核心在于将量子测试仪形式体系与近期提出的紧致克拉默-拉奥型界限相结合。这一表述使我们能够通过可计算半定规划的上界与下界来确定可实现的最高精度。更重要的是，在此框架下，包括纠缠、相干性、量子控制及不定因果序在内的多种量子资源被置于同等地位，并为实现多参数估计的最终精度而进行系统优化。因此，我们的方法适用于存在噪声与无噪声条件下的各种计量策略。为展示其实用性，我们重新审视了三维磁场估计问题，揭示了现有解析结果的优点与局限，并进一步确立了不同类型策略之间的严格层次关系。

Abstract

Precise estimation of physical parameters underpins both scientific discovery and technological development. A central goal of quantum metrology and sensing is to exploit quantum resources like entanglement to devise optimal strategies for estimating physical parameters as precisely as possible. While substantial progress has been made in single-parameter quantum metrology, the multiparameter scenario remains significantly more challenging due to the issue of parameter incompatibility. In this work, we present a unified and computable approach for the simultaneous estimation of multiple parameters that attains the ultimate precision permitted by quantum mechanics. The core of our approach is to integrate the quantum tester formalism into the recently proposed tight Cramér-Rao type bound. This formulation enables us to figure out the highest achievable precision via upper and lower bounds that are computable via semidefinite programs. More importantly, within this formulation, diverse quantum resources, including entanglement, coherence, quantum control, and indefinite causal order, are treated on equal footing and systematically optimized for the purpose of achieving the ultimate precision in multiparameter estimation. As a result, our approach is applicable to various metrological strategies both in the presence and absence of noise. To demonstrate its utility, we revisit three-dimensional magnetic-field estimation, uncovering the strengths and limitations of existing analytical results and further establishing a strict hierarchy among different types of strategies.

Abstract

We address the problem of constructing witnesses for nonclassical light that are applicable in state-of-the-art photon-counting devices. The key ingredient for the criteria we derive are generalized and directly measurable counting statistics and matrices of counting moments. Beyond common criteria, we find classes of witnesses that are based on half-integer powers of click moments and counts. Remarkably, this leads to an exponential increase of the number of nonclassicality criteria one can construct and apply. With this finding, special attention is payed to probing even and odd parity states, requiring such distinct witnesses. Our method is applicable to spatial and time-bin multiplexing in optical systems, where each spatial and temporal mode can be measured with both on-off detectors and detectors with partial internal quasi-photon-number resolution. Generalizations to multimode scenarios are provided, allowing for the direct measurement of nonclassical correlations and coincidence counts between an arbitrary number of modes.

Score: 0.0 / 14.0
Authors: Sumit Chaudhary, Baqir Kazmi, Janis Nötzel

摘要翻译

我们提出一种基于卫星的量子密钥分发网络，该网络能够在全球范围内实现端到端的安全密钥交换，且无需依赖可信中继节点。该网络由环形卫星星座构成，卫星间保持持续互联，并支持两种配置：提供全球覆盖的极轨I型星座，以及提供类地面连续运行的赤道II型星座。端到端保密性通过双场量子密钥分发技术和基于异或运算的冗余密钥转发协议实现，其中每个转发步骤均融合了来自星地链路与星间链路的独立生成量子密钥。因此，最终密钥在任何中间卫星节点均不被暴露，从而消除了可信节点网络中固有的单点脆弱性。网络规模的扩展带来双重优势：安全性的提升与密钥速率的提高。增加星座规模可通过迫使攻击者攻破更多节点以破解协议来增强安全性，同时提升链路可用性与密钥吞吐量。基于实际的上行链路与星间链路模型，我们采用“发送或不发送”双场量子密钥分发协议计算了有限码长下的安全密钥长度。结果表明，可实现的密钥速率随星座规模扩大而显著提升，其中II型星座可实现连续运行并每日生成数千兆比特级密钥，这为构建安全的全球量子通信网络提供了一条可行路径。

Abstract

We propose a satellite-based Quantum Key Distribution (QKD) network that enables global-scale, end-to-end secure key exchange without relying on trusted intermediate nodes. The network is formed by a ring constellation of satellites that maintain persistent inter-satellite connectivity and support two configurations: a polar Type-I constellation providing global coverage, and an equatorial Type-II constellation offering continuous, terrestrial-like operation. End-to-end secrecy is achieved through the use of Twin-field Quantum Key Distribution (TF-QKD) and a redundant XOR-based key-forwarding protocol, in which each forwarding step incorporates independently generated QKD keys from ground-satellite and inter-satellite links. As a result, the final secret key is never exposed to any intermediate satellite, eliminating the single-point vulnerabilities inherent in trusted-node networks. Scaling the network offers two benefits: improved security and higher key rates. Increasing the constellation size enhances security by forcing an adversary to compromise a larger number of nodes to break the protocol, while simultaneously improving link availability and key throughput. Using realistic uplink and Inter-Satellite Link (ISL) models, we compute finite-size secret-key lengths based on the Sending-or-not-sending (SNS)-TF-QKD protocol. Our results show that the achievable key rates scale favourably with constellation size, with Type-II constellations reaching operational continuity and generating multi-gigabit secret keys per day, demonstrating a practical route toward secure global quantum communication.

96. Summing to Uncertainty: On the Necessity of Additivity in Deriving the Born Rule FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 14.0
Authors: Jiaxuan Zhang
Published: 2026-03-06
TL;DR: 该论文研究了量子力学中Born规则推导中可加性假设的必要性，证明该规则不能仅从其他非概率性量子假设推导得出。
摘要翻译

内禀概率的起源长期以来一直是量子力学中最重要且令人困惑的问题之一，而与此问题最直接相关的定律是玻恩定则。一个世纪以来，已有许多尝试将玻恩定则作为定理推导出来，而非将其设定为公设。然而，现有的玻恩定则推导各自基于不同的框架，并引发了不同的批评。它们所依据的假设也高度分化，且彼此间的联系尚未得到充分研究。这些可能的联系很可能是回答量子力学中概率起源问题的关键。 本文着重论证可加性假设在玻恩定则推导中的必要性与不可或缺性。这支持了以下观点：玻恩定则无法仅从其他非概率性的量子力学公设或附加假设中推导出来。我们首先证明，可加性无法从另外两个常用的非概率性附加假设——非语境性与归一化——中推导出来。随后，我们分析了可加性假设在五个现有重要玻恩定则推导中的关键作用。这些推导包括格里森定理、布施对格里森定理的扩展、多伊奇-华莱士定理、祖瑞克的 envariance 证明，以及芬克尔斯坦-哈特定理。我们表明，这些推导要么严重依赖于可加性假设，要么因缺乏可加性而导致明显的漏洞。我们也指出了因缺乏非语境性假设而产生的一些问题。 我们的研究结果为理解可加性假设在量子测量中的重要作用，以及量子力学中概率的起源，提供了新的见解。

Abstract

The emergence of intrinsic probability has long been one of the most important and puzzling problems in quantum mechanics, and the law most directly related to this problem is the Born rule. For a century, there have been many attempts to derive the Born rule as a theorem rather than postulating it. However, existing derivations of the Born rule are each based on different frameworks and have attracted different criticisms. The assumptions from which they start are also highly divergent, and the connections between them have not been sufficiently studied. These possible connections are very likely to be the key to answering questions about the origin of probability in quantum mechanics. This paper focuses on proving the necessity and indispensability of the additivity assumption in the derivation of the Born rule. This supports the view that the Born rule cannot be derived solely from other non-probabilistic quantum or additional postulates. We first prove that additivity cannot be derived from two other commonly used non-probabilistic additional assumptions, non-contextuality and normalization. Then we analyze the crucial role of the additivity assumption in five important existing derivations of the Born rule. These include Gleason's Theorem, Busch's extension of Gleason's Theorem, the Deutsch-Wallace Theorem, Zurek's envariance proof, and the Finkelstein-Hartle Theorem. We show that these derivations either depend heavily on the additivity assumption or lead to obvious loopholes due to the lack of additivity. We also point out some problems arised from the lack of a non-contextuality assumption. Our results provide a novel insight into the important role of additivity assumption in quantum measurement, as well as into the origin of probability in quantum mechanics.

Abstract

Surface ion traps confining and manipulating tens of ion qubits have become the leading platform for quantum processors with high quantum volume. These devices employ the Quantum Charge-Coupled Device (QCCD) architecture, wherein multiple trapping zones are linked by an on-chip transport network that shuttles ion chains, enabling full connectivity through physical ion transport in a plane parallel to the chip surface. The ability to move ions perpendicular to this plane can offer additional advantages, including tuning the laser-ion interaction strength, systematic studies of surface-induced heating mechanisms, and precise alignment with a mode of an external optical cavity. We introduce an "escalator" - a geometrically optimized transition between trapping zones of different confinement heights - and present a comparative analysis of two "elevator" configurations that reposition the RF null dynamically via additional electrode voltages. Both approaches enable nearly a twofold change in the ion confinement height above the chip surface.

TL;DR: 该论文研究了二维费米子匹配门张量网络随机系综与连续场论的关系，发现无序驱动产生了由带拓扑项的非线性sigma模型描述的普适长程行为，建立了随机匹配门网络与热量子霍尔问题的直接对应关系。
摘要翻译

张量网络为量子多体系统提供了离散表示，但其与连续场理论的精确联系仍相对缺乏理解。通过引入典型性概念，我们为具有空间涨落参数的二维费米子匹配门张量网络随机系综建立了连续描述。作为所得普适物理的诊断工具，我们分析了费米子两点函数的无序平均矩，分别在平坦几何和双曲盘上进行研究——其中曲率重塑了其长程结构。我们证明无序驱动了由对称类D的非线性σ模型（含拓扑项）所主导的普适长程行为，这使得随机匹配门网络与热量子霍尔问题直接对应。由此产生的相结构包括局域化相、量子霍尔临界性，以及具有扩散关联和自发复本对称性破缺的鲁棒热金属相。弱非高斯形变将对称性约化为离散置换，为戈德斯通模产生质量，并抑制长程关联。通过这种方式，典型性为从离散张量网络系综到连续量子场理论提供了一条路径。

Abstract

Tensor networks provide discrete representations of quantum many-body systems, yet their precise connection to continuum field theories remains relatively poorly understood. Invoking a notion of typicality, we develop a continuum description for random ensembles of two-dimensional fermionic matchgate tensor networks with spatially fluctuating parameters. As a diagnostic of the resulting universal physics, we analyze disorder-averaged moments of fermionic two-point functions, both in flat geometry and on a hyperbolic disk, where curvature reshapes their long-distance structure. We show that disorder drives universal long-distance behavior governed by a nonlinear sigma-model of symmetry class D with a topological term, placing random matchgate networks in direct correspondence with the thermal quantum Hall problem. The resulting phase structure includes localized phases, quantum Hall criticality, and a robust thermal metal with diffusive correlations and spontaneous replica-symmetry breaking. Weak non-Gaussian deformations reduce the symmetry to discrete permutations, generate a mass for the Goldstone modes, and suppress long-range correlations. In this way, typicality offers a route from ensembles of discrete tensor networks to continuum quantum field theories.

99. Long-range mid-infrared energy transfer mediated by hyperbolic phonon polaritons FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 14.0
Authors: Gonzalo Álvarez-Pérez, Simone De Liberato, Huatian Hu
Published: 2026-03-06
TL;DR: 该论文提出了一个理论框架，证明双曲声子极化激元可以在室温下介导和增强长程中红外能量传输，其传输距离远超传统平台且具有极端方向性。
摘要翻译

我们提出一个理论框架，用以描述单层及扭转二维双曲薄片中的长程能量传递。研究表明，声子极化激元（PhPs，即极性电介质中光子与晶格振动的量子叠加态）能够介导并增强远超过传统中红外（MIR）平台作用范围的室温能量传递，且具有极强的方向性。这是因为偶极-偶极相互作用势能沿实空间双曲开口角的渐近线方向发散。我们的发现使得通常被严格限制在近场范围内的偶极子经典与量子相互作用，得以拓展至数个自由空间中红外波长尺度之外。我们以$α$-MoO$_3$作为代表性材料，但该机制并不局限于中红外波段：它适用于整个电磁频谱范围内的各向异性介质。

Abstract

We provide a framework to theoretically describe long-range energy transfer in single and twisted two-dimensional hyperbolic slabs. We demonstrate that phonon polaritons (PhPs, quantum superpositions of photons and lattice vibrations in polar dielectrics) can mediate and enhance room-temperature energy transfer at ranges far exceeding those of conventional mid-infrared (MIR) platforms, and with extreme directionality. This is because the dipole-dipole interaction potential energy diverges along the asymptotes of the real-space hyperbolic opening angle. Our findings allow us to extend classical and quantum interactions between dipoles, typically strictly confined to the near-field, beyond several free-space MIR wavelengths. We use $α$-MoO$_3$ as a representative material, but this mechanism is not limited to the MIR: it is general to anisotropic media across the whole electromagnetic spectrum.

100. Floquet scars and prethermal fragmentation in a driven spin-one chain FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 14.0
Authors: Krishanu Ghosh, Diptiman Sen, K. Sengupta
Published: 2026-03-06
TL;DR: 该研究通过分析周期性驱动的自旋-1链的Floquet动力学，发现了量子多体疤痕态、热化行为以及在不同驱动频率下出现的预热强/弱希尔伯特空间碎片化现象。
摘要翻译

我们研究了采用振幅为$Q_0$、频率为$ω_D$的方波脉冲协议驱动的自旋-1链的周期动力学。该自旋链的哈密顿量在链节$\ell$上具有热力学大数量的$Z_2$值守恒量$W_{\ell}$。这使得我们能够在具有固定$W_{\ell}$值的给定子空间内研究该链的弗洛凯（Floquet）动力学。对于所有$W_{\ell}=1$的子空间，我们发现在$\hbar ω_D \gg Q_0$条件下存在量子多体疤痕态（quantum many-body scar states）的特征；它们导致特定初始状态下的振荡动力学和保真度复苏。降低$ω_D$后，我们发现了一个遍历性区域，其表现出与（弗洛凯）本征态热化假说预测一致的快速热化。此外，我们识别出特殊的驱动频率$ω_n^{\ast}= Q_0/(2n \hbar)$（其中$n = 1, 2, 3, \cdots$），在这些频率下弗洛凯哈密顿量表现出预热强希尔伯特空间碎片化（strong Hilbert space fragmentation, HSF），其中最大碎片是遍历的；相比之下，在$ω'_n= Q_0/[\hbar(2n+1)]$（其中$n = 0, 1, 2, \cdots$）处则观察到弱希尔伯特空间碎片化（weak HSF）。我们还研究了$W_{\ell} =\{\cdots 1,1,-1,1,1,-1 \cdots \}$的子空间，该子空间在$ω_n^{\ast}$处显示出强HSF，但在$ω'_n$处无碎片化。我们的分析表明，该子空间中的强HSF包含一个可积的最大碎片。我们通过对长度$L\le 24$的有限链进行精确对角化（exact-diagonalization, ED）研究，为我们的解析和微扰结果提供了数值支持。我们关于纠缠熵、保真度以及驱动链关联函数的数值结果，为两个子空间的预热强HSF提供了明确特征。

Abstract

We study the periodic dynamics of a spin-one chain driven using a square-pulse protocol with amplitude $Q_0$ and frequency $ω_D$. The Hamiltonian of the spin chain hosts a thermodynamically large number of $Z_2$-valued conserved quantities $W_{\ell}$ on the links $\ell$. This allows us to study the Floquet dynamics of this chain within a given sector with fixed values of $W_{\ell}$. For the sector with all $W_{\ell}=1$, we find signatures of quantum many-body scar states for $\hbar ω_D \gg Q_0$; they lead to oscillatory dynamics and fidelity revival for specific initial states. Upon lowering $ω_D$, we find an ergodic regime exhibiting fast thermalization consistent with the prediction of the (Floquet) eigenstate thermalization hypothesis. In addition, we identify special drive frequencies $ω_n^{\ast}= Q_0/(2n \hbar)$ (where $n = 1, 2, 3, \cdots$) at which the Floquet Hamiltonian exhibits prethermal strong Hilbert space fragmentation (HSF) with the largest fragment being ergodic; in contrast, a weak HSF is found at $ω'_n= Q_0/[\hbar(2n+1)]$ (where $n = 0, 1, 2, \cdots$). We also study the sector with $W_{\ell} =\{\cdots 1,1,-1,1,1,-1 \cdots \}$ which shows strong HSF at $ω_n^{\ast}$ but no fragmentation at $ω'_n$. Our analysis indicates that the strong HSF in this sector harbors an integrable largest fragment. We provide numerical support for our analytical and perturbative results using exact-diagonalization (ED) studies on finite chains of length $L\le 24$. Our numerical results for entanglement entropy, fidelity, and correlation functions of the driven chain provide definitive signatures of prethermal strong HSF for both sectors.
